                <relative-time datetime="2020-04-23T14:04:58Z" class="no-wrap">Apr 23, 2020</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>In Keras documentation, glorot_uniform says that the initializer is using Glorot Uniform from <a href="http://proceedings.mlr.press/v9/glorot10a/glorot10a.pdf" rel="nofollow">this paper</a>. However, the Keras implementation is totally different from the equation on the paper. Also, there are some arguments such as mode ='fan_avg' is the default. It should be same as the referenced paper. 'fan_sum'. Golort uniform is shown</p>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Alexnet implementation in tensorflow has incomplete architecture where 2 convolution neural layers are missing. This issue is in reference to the python notebook mentioned below.</p>
<p><a href="https://github.com/donnemartin/data-science-ipython-notebooks/blob/master/deep-learning/tensor-flow-examples/notebooks/3_neural_networks/alexnet.ipynb">https://github.com/donnemartin/data-science-ipython-notebooks/blob/master/deep-learning/tensor-flow-examples/notebooks/3_neural_networks/alexnet.ipynb</a></p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"

I tried to build from source, but it's a futile effort.</p>
